Introduction

Documentation pour mon API Laravel.

Base URL: http://localhost

This documentation aims to provide all the information you need to work with our API.

As you scroll, you'll see code examples for working with the API in different programming languages in the dark area to the right (or as part of the content on mobile). You can switch the language used with the tabs at the top right (or from the nav menu at the top left on mobile).

Authenticating requests

This API is not authenticated.

Articles

API pour g√©rer les articles

Lister tous les articles

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost/api/articles" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/articles"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

Example response (200):


[
    {
        "id": 1,
        "nom": "Sample Article",
        "description": "This is a sample article."
    }
]
Received response:
Request failed with error:


Tip: Check that you're properly connected to the network.
If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

Request      

GET api/articles

Headers

Content-Type      

Example: application/json

Accept      

Example: application/json

Store a newly created resource in storage.

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost/api/articles" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"nom\": \"kcgojfmccli\",
    \"description\": \"Et facilis nulla est rerum laborum facilis.\",
    \"ancienPrix\": 286813878.9471,
    \"prix\": 47746,
    \"quantit√©\": 11,
    \"categorieArticle_id\": \"enim\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/articles"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "nom": "kcgojfmccli",
    "description": "Et facilis nulla est rerum laborum facilis.",
    "ancienPrix": 286813878.9471,
    "prix": 47746,
    "quantit√©": 11,
    "categorieArticle_id": "enim"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:


Tip: Check that you're properly connected to the network.
If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

Request      

POST api/articles

Headers

Content-Type      

Example: application/json

Accept      

Example: application/json

Body Parameters

nom   string   

Must not be greater than 255 characters. Example: kcgojfmccli

description   string  optional  

Example: Et facilis nulla est rerum laborum facilis.

ancienPrix   number  optional  

Example: 286813878.9471

prix   number   

Example: 47746

quantit√©   integer   

Example: 11

categorieArticle_id   string   

Example: enim

Display the specified resource.

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost/api/articles/1" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"

    "http://localhost/api/articles/1"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

Update the specified resource in storage.

Example request:

    "http://localhost/api/articles/1" \

    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"nom\": \"vysnektlapuwsgnpqab\",
    \"description\": \"Tempore praesentium alias nisi inventore iure ullam eum repellat.\",
    \"ancienPrix\": 486,
    \"prix\": 815438143.79114,
    \"quantit√©\": 10,
    \"categorieArticle_id\": \"sit\"
}"

GET api/categories

Headers

Content-Type      

Example: application/json

Accept      

Example: application/json

Store a newly created resource in storage.

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost/api/categories" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"nom\": \"oohsjvbpcnnaw\",
    \"description\": \"Est quia sint veritatis nesciunt et sint et et.\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/categories"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "nom": "oohsjvbpcnnaw",
    "description": "Est quia sint veritatis nesciunt et sint et et."
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());

Request      

GET api/categorieArticles

Headers

Content-Type      

Example: application/json

Accept      

Example: application/json

Store a newly created resource in storage.

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost/api/categorieArticles" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"titre\": \"gtzexwsodd\",
    \"article_id\": \"quo\",
    \"categorie_id\": \"molestias\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/categorieArticles"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "titre": "gtzexwsodd",
    "article_id": "quo",
    "categorie_id": "molestias"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());

POST api/images

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost/api/images" \
    --header "Content-Type: multipart/form-data" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --form "titre=yydorbgfegciflooniaoroymp"\
    --form "description=Occaecati ipsam vitae voluptatem laborum."\
    --form "article_id=sed"\
    --form "image=@C:\Users\B\AppData\Local\Temp\php9794.tmp" 
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/images"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "multipart/form-data",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

const body = new FormData();
body.append('titre', 'yydorbgfegciflooniaoroymp');
body.append('description', 'Occaecati ipsam vitae voluptatem laborum.');
body.append('article_id', 'sed');
body.append('image', document.querySelector('input[name="image"]').files[0]);

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body,
}).then(response => response.json());

    --header "Accept: application/json" \

    --form "description=Eligendi iusto aliquid aut quasi est quis."\
    --form "article_id=repellat"\
